Since the taskbar may be frozen:

Press Ctrl + Shift + Esc to open Task Manager.

Find Windows Explorer, right-click it, and choose Restart.

If it's not running, go to File > Run new task, type explorer.exe, and hit Enter.

Spec	Detail
CPU	Intel Core i7-13620H (13th Gen, H-series = high performance) 🔥
GPU	Intel UHD iGPU (No dedicated GPU, not ideal for gaming/VR)
RAM	16 GB DDR4
Storage	512 GB SSD
Display	15.6″ FHD, 60Hz
Weight	1.70 kg
Keyboard	Backlit
Extras	Privacy shutter, MS Office 2024, Windows 11

💥 Strengths
✅ 13th Gen i7-H is a very powerful CPU — significantly stronger than the Ryzen 7 7530U/7730U in raw performance (especially in burst workloads like compiling code, multitasking, etc.)

✅ Good for future-proofing, ML experimentation, dev work

✅ Decent build for mid-tier ASUS laptops

✅ Full-size screen with backlit keyboard

✅ Best if your tasks involve processing-heavy tools (Android Studio, VS Code + emulator, AI notebooks)

⚠️ Weak Spots
❌ Only integrated graphics (iGPU) → not suitable for Unity, 3D, VR, or Blender work

❌ Battery life on H-series CPUs is typically worse than U-series (expect 3.5–5 hours vs 7+ on Lenovo Slim 5)

❌ Weaker display compared to Slim 5’s 300 nits IPS

❌ Build quality isn't as premium as Lenovo Slim 5 (Lenovo’s chassis is MIL-STD grade and lighter)

🧠 My Verdict (Straight Talk):
Category	Winner
Raw CPU Power	✅ ASUS i7-13620H
Battery Life	🔋 Lenovo Slim 5
Build Quality	🛡️ Lenovo Slim 5
Display Quality	🎨 Lenovo Slim 5
Thermals/Fan Noise	🔇 Lenovo is quieter
Weight & Portability	🧳 Lenovo is lighter (1.46 kg vs 1.70 kg)
Future-Proof for VR, AI, Dev	🤝 ASUS (for CPU), Lenovo (for balance)

[30/07/25, 9:57:49 PM] Suraj Vidya School Classmate: To,
The Principal,
Vidya School,
Gurgaon.

Subject: Application for Scholarship

Respected Ma'am,

With due respect, I would like to state that I am an ex-student of your esteemed school. I belong to a financially weak family. My father is not with us anymore and my mother is the only earning member of my family. Her monthly income is only 8,000 rupees. It is very difficult for her to manage our household expenses and my higher education alone with this income.

I am sincere and dedicated towards my studies. I want to make my mother proud and secure a good future for my family. I am glad to inform you that I have recently got admission in Gurugram University for B.Tech (CSE AI) and I have managed to pay my first semester fees with great difficulty. But due to my weak financial condition, it is not possible for us to pay the remaining fees and other educational expenses.

Therefore, I humbly request you to kindly grant me a scholarship so that I can continue my higher studies without any financial burden on my mother. I assure you that I will always study with dedication and make my school proud.

I shall be highly grateful to you for your kind support and help.

Thanking you,

Yours obediently,
Suraj Singh Chauhan
Course: B.Tech (CSE AI)
Contact No.: 8700080399
